<td style="width: 11%"><b>Item 8.01</b></td><td style="width: 89%"><b>Other Events.</b></td></tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">On October&#160;8, 2024, Rockwell Medical,&#160;Inc.,
a Delaware corporation (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Company</span>&#8221;), filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">SEC</span>&#8221;)
a shelf registration statement on Form&#160;S-3 (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">New Registration Statement</span>&#8221;) to replace the existing shelf registration
statement on Form&#160;S-3 (No.&#160;333-259923) filed with the SEC on September&#160;30, 2021 (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Prior Registration Statement</span>&#8221;),
which was scheduled to expire on October&#160;8, 2024, pursuant to Rule&#160;415(a)(5)&#160;under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended.
The Prior Registration Statement was deemed terminated upon the effectiveness of the New Registration Statement on October&#160;21, 2024.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">In connection with the filing of the New Registration
Statement, on November&#160;13, 2024, the Company filed a prospectus supplement (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Prospectus Supplement</span>&#8221;) covering
the offer and sale of an aggregate offering price of up to $25,000,000 of the Company&#8217;s common stock, par value $0.0001 per share
(the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Common Stock</span>&#8221;), pursuant to the Controlled Equity Offering<sup>SM</sup> Sales Agreement, dated April&#160;8,
2022 (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Sales Agreement</span>&#8221;), by and between Cantor Fitzgerald&#160;&amp; Co. and the Company. A copy of the Sales
Agreement was previously filed as Exhibit&#160;10.2 to the Company&#8217;s Annual Report on Form&#160;10-K with the SEC on March&#160;21,
2024.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">The Company is filing this Current Report on Form&#160;8-K
to provide the legal opinion of its counsel, Gibson, Dunn&#160;&amp; Crutcher LLP, regarding the legality of the securities covered by
the Prospectus Supplement, which opinion is attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;5.1.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Ladies and Gentlemen:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">We have examined the Registration Statement on
Form&nbsp;S-3 (File No.&nbsp;333-282538) (the &ldquo;<U>Registration Statement</U>&rdquo;) of Rockwell Medical,&nbsp;Inc., a Delaware
corporation (the &ldquo;<U>Company</U>&rdquo;), filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &ldquo;<U>Commission</U>&rdquo;)
on October&nbsp;8, 2024, pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (the &ldquo;<U>Securities Act</U>&rdquo;), and the prospectus
supplement thereto dated November&nbsp;13, 2024 (the &ldquo;<U>Prospectus Supplement</U>&rdquo;), in connection with the offering by the
Company of up to $25,000,000 of the Company&rsquo;s common stock, par value $0.0001 per share (the &ldquo;<U>Shares</U>&rdquo;).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">In arriving at the opinion expressed below, we
have examined originals, or copies certified or otherwise identified to our satisfaction as being true and complete copies of the originals,
of specimen Common Stock certificates and such other documents, corporate records, certificates of officers of the Company and of public
officials and other instruments as we have deemed necessary or advisable to enable us to render the opinions set forth below. In our examination,
we have assumed without independent investigation the genuineness of all signatures, the legal capacity and competency of all natural
persons, the authenticity of all documents submitted to us as originals and the conformity to original documents of all documents submitted
to us as copies. We have further assumed that all offers and sales of the Shares will comply with the minimum offering price and pricing
formula set forth in the authorization of the offering and sale of the Shares by the Company&rsquo;s Board of Directors.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Based upon the foregoing, and subject to the assumptions,
exceptions, qualifications and limitations set forth herein, we are of the opinion that the Shares, when issued against payment therefor
as set forth in the Registration Statement and the Prospectus Supplement thereto, will be validly issued, fully paid and non-assessable.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">We consent to the filing of this opinion as an
exhibit to the Registration Statement, and we further consent to the use of our name under the caption &ldquo;Legal Matters&rdquo; in
the Registration Statement and the Prospectus Supplement. In giving these consents, we do not thereby admit that we are within the category
of persons whose consent is required under Section&nbsp;7 of the Securities Act or the Rules&nbsp;and Regulations of the Commission.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Very truly yours,</P>
